Qingjiang

Qingjiang-Suqian Buses Temporarily Unable to Travel Directly 100

The buses traveling from Qingjiang to Suqian used to travel directly between the two stations, with one bus each day, which was convenient for passengers. Recently, due to the upper reaches of the abandoned Yellow River channel in the middle of the route being flooded, the water is five or six feet deep, no longer allowing passage through the river center as before. This river is located between Siyang County and Zhongyu, so the vehicles traveling from Qingjiang only reach Zhongxing, and the vehicles coming from Suqian only reach Siyang. Passengers from both sides must cross the abandoned Yellow River to transfer vehicles to Qingjiang and Suqian. Therefore, in order to facilitate both Qingjiang and Suqian, they use the Qingjiang-Siyang bus to transfer passengers to Pu every day, and at the same time use the Suqian-Siyang bus to transfer passengers to Suqian. Back and forth, both stations use the original bus to run twice, in order to maintain current traffic. However, it is much more inconvenient than before.

Pinghu

County Government Strictly Urges Defense Corps Donations 101

Since its establishment, the county's Defense Corps has made great contributions to safeguarding the area during the winter defense. However, donations have been sporadic, making it difficult to fund. Last year, stores such as Qichun Pavilion asked to be abolished because they could not afford it. At that time, a certain gentleman from the county party headquarters encouraged them, saying that from the second half of the 23rd year of the Republic of China, he would find a way to reduce it appropriately. Therefore, from July of this year, the stores delayed paying donations. The county government's tax collectors repeatedly urged them without success. The day before yesterday, when the tax collector went to Qichun Pavilion to collect donations, the store owner Shao Xueling stated that he would not pay without a reduction. He also said that if he insisted on collecting donations, he could collect them from the county party headquarters. The tax collector returned to the government and reported the facts. County Magistrate Zhang became furious and immediately signed a warrant ordering the store owner Shao to be brought to justice. The Chamber of Commerce heard about it and Fang and Zhang went to see him to intercede for Shao. The County Magistrate said that Shao not only resisted donations, but also used such wording to public officials, which was absurd. This time, the stores' resistance to donations was found to be instigated by Shao. Since he was causing trouble, he would be sent to the Provincial Security Office for investigation. Fang and others agreed and left. It is now reported that the store is willing to pay the three months of unpaid donations, and the unpaid donations of all stores will also be paid in full.

Hangzhou

Freight Train Runs Over Elderly Woman 102

Yesterday afternoon, a Shanghai-Hangzhou freight train was traveling from Shanghai to Hangzhou. When it reached Nanxing Station, a woman named Wu, 69 years old, who lived in Fengshanmen, was carrying a basket of noodles home from Nanxing Bridge. When she was crossing the tracks, the train arrived and it was too late to avoid her. She was knocked down and both legs were crushed, leaving a bloody mess. The railway police hired a car to rush her to the hospital for treatment. She died shortly after due to old age and excessive blood loss. The local court was notified to send officials to examine and coffin the body.

Illegal Extortion Handed Over to the Province for Strict Handling 103

Huang Guoji, a patrol officer of the Pinghu County Public Security Bureau, and Wu Lufu, a police chief, illegally extorted money from arrested opium offenders for their release. After someone reported it to the Civil Affairs Department of the Provincial Government, it sent personnel to secretly investigate and confirmed the facts. The patrol officer, the police chief, and others were escorted to the province and handed over to the court for strict handling in accordance with the law.

Letter from the Chief of the Third Branch of the Jiashan County Public Security Bureau 104

Dear Editor, I was surprised to read an article in your newspaper's "County News" section on the 27th of this month entitled "Villagers in Jiashan Petition for the Removal of Wu Yue." According to reports, at 7:00 PM on the 25th of this month, Shen Lantai, the chief of the Didian Township in this area, was heavily involved in gambling and skimming profits. He requested that the police be sent to arrest him. The chief of this branch, for the sake of caution, led the chief police to investigate and arrest him. Two gamblers, Shen Rongqing and others, and gambling equipment were caught on the spot. Just as they were about to be taken to the bureau, fifteen or sixteen shots of wooden shell guns were fired from the roof of the township chief's house. The chief of this branch went out to investigate, but the shooter escaped in the darkness. At 8:00 AM on the 26th, following the county government's telegram order, he went to investigate with the core team. At that time, four gambling offenders, including Shen Santuan and others, were arrested and taken to the bureau and have now been sentenced. The shooter, Shen Qiada, is at large. The details have been reported to the county bureau and the county government for verification. As for the so-called "sending clothes to catch gamblers," "searching the entire village," "hitting the township chief with the butt of a gun," "injuring him all over," "gathering crowds to protest," and "villagers petitioning," all of these are not true. I am deeply concerned that this may confuse the audience and greatly affect the reputation of our bureau and the chief of the branch. Therefore, I am writing to request a correction to show the truth. Sincerely, Wu Yue, Chief of the Third Branch of the Jiashan County Public Security Bureau. October 28th.

Page 13

Local News

Hai Yuan New Ship Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday Afternoon 105

Arrived at Songkou at 1 PM and Docked at Gaochang Temple at 3 PM

First Voyage to Guangzhou and Hong Kong Scheduled for the 12th

The state-owned China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's newly built Hai Yuan ship in England arrived in Shanghai yesterday afternoon and docked at the Jiangnan Shipyard Wharf in Gaochang Temple. It will be sailed into the dry dock this morning for inspection of its machinery. The ship's crew has also been assigned by the company. After formal acceptance, it will sail to Guangzhou and Hong Kong for the first time on the morning of the 12th. The Hai Ting and Hai Li ships have also been completed and sailed to China, while the Hai Zhen ship is still under construction. Approximately one ship will arrive at the port every three weeks. The details are as follows:

Construction Process 106

In order to develop its business, the state-owned China Merchants Steam Navigation Company borrowed 400,000 pounds from the Central Boxer Indemnity Committee to build four seagoing vessels. After approval by the Ministry of Transportation, it signed a contract with the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Committee and drafted designs. The bidding and construction in England went smoothly. The four ships all have a deadweight tonnage of more than 3,000 tons. The Hai Yuan and Hai Li ships were built by Swan Hunter & Wigham Richardson & Co. in Newcastle, while the Hai Ting and Hai Zhen ships were built by Barclay Curle & Co. in Glasgow. Both factories have a long-standing reputation in the British shipbuilding industry.

Voyage to China 107

The Hai Yuan wheel, estimated to weigh 3,200 tons, was the first to be built. It was launched on July 20th of this year, with the wife of our country's Minister to the UK, Guo Taiqi, performing the bottle-throwing ceremony. The interior engineering was completed on September 13th, and it departed from England the following day, driven by the construction company to Shanghai for delivery. Two engineers, Huang Zonglun and Li Changwen, who were sent by the China Merchants Bureau for practical training, returned to the country with the ship. After leaving England, the ship traveled at a speed of ten knots per hour (approximately 33 Chinese miles) non-stop. It passed the Strait of Gibraltar on September 21st, arrived in Port Said on the 29th, contacted the Suez Canal Company, and crossed the canal the next day. It passed Aden on October 6th, Colombo on the 15th, Singapore on the 21st, and Hong Kong on the 27th. It finally arrived at the Wusongkou at 1:00 PM yesterday, covering a total distance of approximately 18,000 nautical miles in 48 days.

Import Yesterday Afternoon 108

After the Hai Yuan wheel arrived at Wusongkou at 1:00 PM yesterday, the China Merchants Bureau dispatched a pre-hired pilot to guide it into the port. It passed the Huazhan at 1:30 PM and the Bund at 2:30 PM. The ship sounded its whistle in salute to the bureau's entrance, and the bureau's staff gathered on the balcony to watch. The ship sailed directly to the Jiangnan Shipyard at Gaochangmiao, mooring at the dock at approximately 3:00 PM. The bureau specially sent the Deputy Director of Shipping, Zhao Yuntai, to welcome it.

Crew Arriving in Shanghai 109

The voyage to China was the responsibility of the construction company. The ship's crew consisted of eight British individuals, including the captain, first mate, second mate, telegraph operator, and four engineers. In addition to Huang and Li, the Chinese crew members returning to the country, there were also eight Chinese laborers temporarily hired in the Netherlands as stokers, four sailors, and four assistants. After arriving in Shanghai, all Chinese and foreign crew members were either given funds to disband or return to their respective countries by the company.

A Glimpse of the New Ship 110

The new ship was flying the national flags of China and England, as well as the international flag, which was quite a magnificent sight. The ship was 343 feet long, 47 feet wide, 25 feet high to the upper deck, and 17 feet 6 inches high to the main deck. It had a carrying capacity of 3,200 tons. The bottom of the ship was painted red, the hull was painted black, and inlaid with red lines. The words "Hai Yuan" were made of bronze-colored metal and placed on both sides of the ship's waist, which was very eye-catching. The outer layers of the cabins were painted white, and the interior had eleven large dining rooms, twenty-two passenger seats, sixteen official cabins, and fifty-three passenger seats. The rest were economy class passenger seats. The layout of each department was magnificent and the equipment was also very perfect.

Mr. Li's Interview 111

According to Mr. Li Changwen, who returned with the ship, speaking to a reporter from the Central News Agency on board, "We were sent to British shipyards for practical training, and there were six of us in total, including naval architects Huang Zonglun, machine engineers Zhang Guoquan, Shi Ruichang, and myself, as well as Zhou Yanjin and Wang Chengzhu, two graduates from the merchant marine school. Our group of people departed from Shanghai on May 19th and arrived in London on the afternoon of June 23rd. We were designated by the China Merchants Bureau's new ship construction supervision committee members, Wu Daming and Shi Gan, with myself and Huang and Wang to practice at the Newcastle shipyard, and Zhang, Zhou, and Shi to practice at the Glasgow shipyard. The Hai Yuan wheel was launched on July 27th, with Mrs. Guo, the Minister's wife, performing the bottle-throwing ceremony. It was completed on September 13th and departed for China on the 14th. Mr. Huang and I returned to the country with the ship. The weather was not good along the way, and there were no major storms. We did not stop at any ports along the way except for Port Said, because Port Said is the northern entrance to the Suez Canal, and ships crossing the river must first contact the canal company, so it was necessary to stop. This trip took a total of 48 days. The other three ships have also been completed one after another, and one ship can arrive in Shanghai every three weeks thereafter."

Overseas Chinese Not Onboard 112

The Hai Yuan wheel going to the Netherlands to carry unemployed overseas Chinese back to the country was mandated by central and Ministry of Transportation telegrams. Therefore, when entering the port at Wusong, the bureau still claimed that there were more than one hundred overseas Chinese from the Netherlands coming aboard. When the ship arrived at the Jiangnan factory, it was learned that not a single person was onboard. The reason for not carrying them was that when the Hai Yuan wheel left England for Shanghai, the shipbuilding commissioner stationed in the UK received another telegram from Minister Zhu, instructing the wheel to go to the Netherlands to load a large number of overseas Chinese (a total of more than 500 people) returning to the country. However, at that time, the Hai Yuan had not yet been handed over to the bureau. The British captain, who was responsible for driving the ship to Shanghai, believed that because the contracted price was limited, the ship would need to use more coal if it sailed to the Netherlands, and there was no use for a large number of Chinese on board, as there was no large amount of money paid. Therefore, he refused to go to the Netherlands to carry them, causing a large number of overseas Chinese to look forward to it in the Netherlands, but they were never able to return to the country. When the ship sailed, the German embassy sent a letter requesting that several overseas Chinese be carried back, but because the power was in the hands of the British (who managed the entire ship), it could not be done. However, this intention was not telegraphed to Shanghai to clarify, causing the bureau to believe that there were overseas Chinese coming along.

Assignment of Crew Members 113

The bureau originally advocated hiring Chinese shipmasters for the new ship. However, because the ship had to pass through Hong Kong, it was only allowed to enter the port if examined by the Hong Kong authorities. And, because the ship needed to set sail urgently, it was decided by the bureau affairs meeting to temporarily employ foreign shipmasters. Captain Jonathan of the Xin Jiangtian ship was transferred to fill the position. Chen Bangda was appointed as the first mate, Liu Chuansen as the second mate, Xu Hanqing as the third mate, and the engine captain was hired from England for a fixed term of six months. Ni Shunlai was the first engineer, Zheng Rongfa the second engineer, and Yan Yi the third engineer. All have been assigned and will take office after acceptance.

Scheduled Departure 114

The Hai Yuan wheel is scheduled to enter the dry dock this morning. The bureau will send personnel to inspect the machinery and repaint the hull. It is scheduled to dock at the Jinliyuan Wharf on the 10th of this month to hold an acceptance ceremony, while inviting Chinese and foreign guests to visit. The next day, it will host merchants and people from all walks of life to visit at the same location. It is also scheduled to sail to Hong Kong and Guangdong for the first time on the morning of the 12th, and dock at You Tou and other ports. In the future, it will sail once every two weeks, carrying both passengers and cargo.

Sinking of Hai Ping Steamer of Haichang Company 115

Total Loss of Ship and Cargo

Company Received Telegram Yesterday

Truth Being Thoroughly Investigated

Haichang Steamship Company, located on Rue du Consulat, French Concession, owns the Hai Shun, Hai Ping, and Hai Chang wheels, operating between Shanghai and Yingkou. After the Hai Ping wheel went from Shanghai to Yingkou last time, it docked at the South Manchuria Railway Company Wharf, loaded with 2,200 tons of Fushun coal. At approximately 9:00 AM yesterday, because it was fully loaded, it sailed from Yingkou, bound for Shanghai. It was originally scheduled to arrive at the port for unloading on November 6th.

Sunk in Collision Unexpectedly, Hai Ping lifted anchor at 9:30 AM yesterday, leaving the wharf. Just as it was starting up, a tanker from the Asiatic Petroleum Company approached the Hai Ping wheel. The wheel failed to avoid it, causing the mid-ship to be violently struck by the Asiatic wheel. It immediately breached, and water poured in. Because it was heavily loaded, it sank within minutes.

Total Loss of Ship and Cargo The Hai Ping wheel sank outside the South Manchuria Wharf. The 2,200 tons of Fushun coal in the hold also went into the port with the wheel. Fortunately, there were no passengers in the hold. All the crew members, because they were close to the wharf after the accident, were able to escape to shore, but everyone's personal and private belongings were lost and could not be retrieved.

Reported to Shanghai The owner of the Haichang Steamship is Zhu Zhe, the first mate is Tang Zhuangxing, the second mate is Song Yuanjian, and the comprador is Liu Zhenxi. Haichang Company in Shanghai received a telegram from shipowner Zhu Zhe and the Yingkou branch yesterday afternoon, and telegraphed to Yingkou overnight to inquire about the truth of the collision, requesting a detailed report.

A Glimpse of the Loss The Hai Ping wheel has a capacity of 2,600 tons and travels the Shanghai-Beiyang line. The wheel has 120,000 yuan of marine insurance in various companies of the Joint Shipping Insurance Association. Yesterday afternoon, the company received the news and notified various insurance companies, and also notified the coal owners. The insurance company must conduct a detailed investigation of the collision to determine the responsibility for the accident. As for the loss of cargo, the ship and the belongings and luggage of the crew, the loss is estimated at around 200,000 yuan.

New Stamps Will Be Affixed Starting Today, and Old Regulations Still Apply 119

Old Stamps Cannot Be Affixed Again, Awaiting Registration for Exchange

New Stamp Tax Law Has Been Passed But Not Yet Implemented

The new pagoda-shaped stamps printed by the Ministry of Finance will be available for sale at post offices across the country starting today. However, regarding this matter, merchants in this city have a misunderstanding that the new stamp tax law will also be implemented on the same day, causing businesses to repeatedly call the Municipal General Chamber of Commerce yesterday to inquire. Now, Yan Esheng, Secretary of the Municipal General Chamber of Commerce, officially issued the following explanation:

Regulations Valid 120

It has been found that the stamps currently affixed are handled in accordance with the Provisional Stamp Tax Regulations of the National Government of the Republic of China. The regulations consist of nine articles, dividing the stamped items into four categories, including fifteen types in the first category, fourteen types in the second category, forty-five types in the third category, and four types in the fourth category, for a total of seventy-eight types. The new stamp tax law passed by the Legislative Yuan has not yet been promulgated and implemented by the National Government, and chambers of commerce in various places are striving to amend it, so it cannot be applied, of course.

Old Stamps Registration 121

As for the original old stamp tax stamps, the Municipal General Chamber of Commerce fought for exchanging the old for the new to the Ministry, and the Ministry of Finance has approved it. After registration, the new stamps will be exchanged in installments, but the registration and exchange methods are being drafted by the Ministry of Finance and have not yet been announced. Recently, the Municipal General Chamber of Commerce also telegraphed to urge the prompt promulgation. But what can be said is that old stamps cannot be affixed from November 1st. However, they are not discarded, and after the Ministry of Finance promulgates the registration method, the new stamps will be exchanged in installments.

No Need to Re-paste 122

Affixing new stamps from November 1st refers to newly created vouchers. If old vouchers have already been pasted with old stamps, there is no need to re-paste new stamps. For example, if this year's account book has already been pasted with old stamps at the beginning of the year, it is of course still valid and can be pasted with new stamps at the beginning of the following year after the end of the year, which has been clearly instructed by the Ministry of Finance by telegram.

Inspection Method 123

From November 1st, after the new stamps are sold by the post office, all matters related to the inspection of stamps will be handled by the governments of each province, city, and county. Personnel will be dispatched by the provincial stamp, tobacco, and alcohol tax bureaus to conduct random inspections at any time. Cases of violations of the stamp tax regulations will be handled by local judicial organs. The Stamp Tax Case Review Committee established previously also ended at the end of October. However, matters related to the inspection of stamps in the Shanghai Concession have always been handled by the Concession Investigation Department and sent to the court for trial. From November 1st, they will continue to be handled as before without any changes.

Answers to Questions 124

Since stamp tax cases will be tried by the court in the future, it is necessary to study carefully the interpretation of the stamp tax regulations to decide what should be pasted and what does not need to be pasted,

Page 14

instead of having the former Review Committee consider the circumstances and handle them leniently. The Municipal General Chamber of Commerce Commercial Monthly has compiled a book of answers to questions about stamp tax, containing various instructions, approvals, and interpretations of the Ministry of Finance and the Stamp Tax Bureau on stamp tax issues, which is very detailed. The content includes 84 clauses and also includes the full text of the Provisional Regulations. Each book is sold for only 15 cents, which is the most accurate reference book on stamp tax.

Shipping Association Appeals for Pilotage Matters 125

Please Order the Customs Not to Impose Non-Closing Penalties Again

Pilots Went to Beijing Last Night to Petition the Court

After the China Pilot Management Committee announced the Song-Han Pilot Regulations, the Jianghai Customs implemented a refusal to unqualified pilots. The shipping companies gathered to discuss the matter and decided to suspend operations and telegraphed an appeal. A joint pilot petition group went to Beijing last night to petition. The details are recorded as follows:

Management Committee Announcement 126

Ke Fair, Director of the Song-Han District Pilot Office, announced: "1. From October 1, 1934, all personnel are under the jurisdiction of this Management Committee. Without the permission of this Management Committee, they may not accept contract employment from any shipping company. Please pay attention. When this office sends a pilot out to serve, it fills out a pilot dispatch form. When the ship is closed, please take this form and the practice certificate to the Shanghai Port Affairs Bureau for verification. 2. To whom it may concern, all personnel are under the jurisdiction of this Management Committee as short-term pilots. If anyone comes to this office, please report to the registry."

Shipping Association Appeal 127

The shipping companies decided that before the Jianghai Customs has resolved the agreement between the two parties, it must appoint the pilot of the Pilot Management Committee, otherwise it will not be allowed to close the customs. Therefore, after the suspension of operations, the Shipping Association has drafted a telegram yesterday, which was sealed by Chairman Yu Qiaqing, and will be telegraphed to the Central Party Headquarters, the National Government, and the Executive Yuan today, requesting the Customs not to impose penalties for non-closure until the agreement between the two parties has been resolved. At the same time, the letter was sent to the Inspector General of Customs for inspection.

Pilot Petition 128

Zhang Ruiqing and 56 other pilots who failed the examination of the China Pilot Management Committee all hold licenses from the Naval Pilot Training Institute. They organized the Song-Han Joint Pilot Petition Group and yesterday appointed representatives Feng Yuqing, Zhang Zicong, and Zhang Fu, and ten others to bring a presentation and took the Shanghai-Nanjing night express to Beijing at 11:00 PM last night to petition the Central Party Headquarters, the Ministry of Finance, the Ministry of Industry, and the Ministry of the Navy. It was also decided that Zhang Ruiqing would be appointed as a representative to petition the Shanghai Special Municipal Party Headquarters and the Municipal Government today.

Petition Content 129

The petition is to maintain the shipping industry, protect livelihoods, restore national rights, and prevent foreigners from trampling on them in disguise. I believe that the pilotage of various ports in our country has been almost entirely occupied by foreigners, and now if there is only a remaining part, it is only the Yangtze River line. Looking at modern countries, there is hardly an example of allowing foreigners to serve as pilots within its territory. Although the lives of the representatives who serve as Yangtze River pilots have never been slightly affected by foreign forces, they have long been saddened by the sight of foreign forces infringing on navigation rights. Recently, the establishment of the Pilot Management Committee has given the power to foreigners from the Customs. First, the pilots in our Song-Han District have been ravaged and arbitrarily acted, illegally revoking the qualifications of the representatives, monopolizing shipping affairs, and trying to gradually erode the navigation rights of the Yangtze River inland waterway, so as to expand their imperialist forces and try to annex China. The representatives are concerned about their livelihoods and the national rights. In addition to the petitions that have been submitted to the Yuan requesting assistance in saving the case, representatives were specially sent to the Yuan for petitions, and it is requested that the petition be examined and transferred for prevention (omitted). In short, if the Pilot Management Committee allows foreigners to visit, the brutality of foreigners will be more unbridled. This will not only harm the livelihoods of the pilots in our Song-Han District and suffer from their poison, but also be a conspiracy by foreigners and a unilateral act of the country. If it is not quickly stopped, national rights will not be guaranteed. The representatives are forced to jointly present the details of the situation, requesting examination and rapid prevention of the illegal acts of the Pilot Management Committee, and asking for rescue.

Shipowners as Pilots 130

Since the Chunhe wheel of the Hefeng Steamship Company was refused closure by the Jianghai Customs because the pilot was unqualified, yesterday, the Tongli wheel of the Zhengji Steamship Company sailed from Tianjin to Jiangyin with cargo. Two Announcements from Jianghai Customs 131

Regulations on Taxable Goods in Luggage

Restrictions on Passengers Carrying Silver Dollars and Copper Coins

Tang Haian, Superintendent of the Jianghai Customs, and Berlede, Commissioner of Customs, issued joint announcements yesterday. They are recorded as follows: (1) For the purpose of complying with the order to stipulate that the import tax on taxable goods carried in passengers' luggage is limited to one gold unit and the export tax is limited to two national currencies, and the transit tax for domestic travel is exempted if it is less than five national currencies, Announcement No. 1395. In accordance with the order of the Ministry of Finance, it is hereby stipulated that the minimum amount of tax levied by the customs baggage inspection team on taxable goods carried in passengers' luggage is one gold unit for import tax and one national currency for export tax per passenger, and that all amounts less than this amount shall be exempted. As for taxable items in luggage traveling to various commercial ports in China, if the amount of transit tax per passenger is less than five national currencies, they will be exempted from taxation, etc. This shall be complied with and notified to all merchants. (2) For the purpose of complying with the order to revise the limited number of copper coins and silver coins carried by passengers, Announcement No. 1393. According to the order of the Ministry of Finance, the original stipulation of 10,000 single copper coins per passenger has now been changed to 5,000 coins, and the original stipulation that silver coins, whether single or double, that are not inferior or light coins, whose number is within 500 coins, is allowed for merchants to transport freely, is now changed to within 300 coins, which is allowed for merchants to transport freely. This shall be complied with and notified to all merchants.

Owners of Various Industries in This City Oppose Landlords Paying Donations for Tenants 132

Not Only Does It Not Conform to the Regulations

And it Adds Many Losses

The Municipal Finance Bureau previously issued a public notice that the housing donation for residential houses will be revised to 12% of the rent, which will still be borne half by the landlord and half by the tenant. However, if the tenant delays in paying the housing donation in the future, the landlord shall be responsible for paying it, and the donation paid on behalf of the tenant shall be offset when collecting the rent, etc., as seen in the previous report. Now the owners in the two districts of Shanghai South and Zhabei believe that the above-mentioned notice is inconsistent with the revised housing donation rules published by the municipal government. Citizens Wu Baodi, Xu Zuoliang, Wang Binyan, Shen Lianfang, Wang Ling, Yao Ziruo, Gu Lugui, Jia Jiying, Yu Baojing, Ling Bohua, Mao Jingchou, Zhang Yi, etc., jointly petitioned the Finance Bureau to revoke it. The original text reads: "The petition is that the landlord has no obligation to pay the housing donation for the tenant in arrears. It is sincerely hoped that it will be revoked quickly to conform to the regulations and show fairness. On September 30th of this year, 12% will be collected according to the rent, which will still be borne half by the owner and half by the tenant. It is also stipulated that if the tenant delays in paying the housing donation in the future, the landlord shall be responsible for paying it, and the donation paid on behalf of the tenant shall be offset when collecting the rent, etc., which is surprising. It has been found that the market has declined in recent years, and the social economy has suddenly become exhausted. The rent reduction movement of tenants is like a whirlwind. The difficulty in collecting rent from landlords is also a pressing issue. In such a situation, we hope that the government authorities will sympathize with the difficulties of the people and reduce the donation rate to provide relief. However, reading this notice, the housing donation for residential houses must be increased by 2% starting this winter. The citizens know that they cannot afford to take on the burden at this time, but since it has been approved by the central government, even if they object, it will be ineffective, so they have to remain silent in pain. The only consolation is that the landlord and tenant each bear half of the housing donation, and the half that the landlord should pay is paid by the tenant and deducted from the rent that should be paid, which is clearly stated in Article 11 of the revised rules for collecting housing donations published by the Shanghai Municipal Government. Since its implementation, it has been quite convenient, and the tenant has no loss in paying the half of the housing donation on behalf of the landlord because the rent can be deducted. As for whether the tenant's donation is delayed, it depends entirely on whether the collector's collection is effective or not. The landlord is absolutely not responsible. If the loss of the tenant's arrears is made the responsibility of the landlord, it is not only inconsistent with the regulations, but the collector will definitely not be willing to do his best to collect the donation. Because the housing donation owed by the tenant will be compensated by the landlord in the future, there is no need to urge the tenant to pay it. Although the notice states that the donation paid on behalf of the tenant shall be offset when collecting the rent, it is not known that the police are assisting in the collection of housing donations, and the public power is the backing. Even for tenants who cannot afford to pay, they have to be allowed to delay. If they delay the donation to the public, they must owe a lot of rent. How can the landlord pay for them again? If the tenant escapes for this reason, from whom will the compensation be obtained? As a result, the landlord will incur many losses. We owners cannot remain silent in the face of such an obligation. Therefore, we jointly petition the Yuan Bureau to review it and quickly issue an order to revoke the section in this notice regarding the tenant's delayed payment of the housing donation, which requires the landlord to pay it and offset it when collecting the rent, so as to conform to the regulations and show fairness.

Various districts of Shanghai County suffered from drought in the summer of this year and were damaged by wind, rain, and snow. Although the river basin area has been rescued by rental machines, it is still not fruitful due to the lack of rain. The mountainous areas and fields far from the riverbanks are even more unable to be irrigated due to the drying up of ditches and ponds, resulting in no harvest. According to the survey results, the total disaster area in the county is about 70% or more, and the loss is more than 8 million yuan. The total number of disaster victims is more than 210,000. Therefore, the articles and telegrams requesting relief from various villages and towns are coming in one after another, and the representatives pleading for relief are constantly on the road. We think that our county is located near the Beijing-Shanghai Railway and was originally known for its poverty. In recent years, disasters have continued to occur, and the vitality of the rural areas has been almost lost. Since this year's severe drought, the livelihood of the poor has been cut off, and the lack of food and starvation are now heard every day. The state of displacement and wandering is unbearable to witness. Alas, the fertile fields have all become red land, and the remnants of the people will become starving corpses. This is truly an unprecedented disaster in a hundred years and the greatest catastrophe for the people. In the blink of an eye, the cold winter is approaching, and hunger and cold will come together. If we do not seek relief urgently, the weak will have no one to turn to and will die, and the brave will take risks, which may hinder public security. Although we have repeatedly reported the situation to the provincial government, we have first issued urgent relief to help them. However, the disaster area this year is vast, and the provincial treasury is limited. The construction compensation is intended to replace relief with work, which is also a slow solution. Jingqian is unable to perform his duties and lacks the means to provide relief. He is making a call for help to celebrate the hope of recovery. We have always admired □□'s warm concern and have been troubled by the suffering of the people. We have specially detailed the disaster situation, hoping to show compassion for the hungry people who are crying and begging in the fields, and generously issue food and clothing to prolong their lives. Then, not only will the re-creators pray with incense, but also those who are in charge of the pastoral care will also be grateful beyond measure. We respectfully submit this letter and hope that you will consider it.

Ministry of Interior Appoints Pan Xulun as Accountant for Red Cross Audit 145

And Orders Ten Audit Regulations

Since the Red Cross Society of the Republic of China passed a resolution at this year's provincial representatives' conference to reorganize the administrative department, everything has been progressing actively. The Ministry of Interior also attaches great importance to the society's affairs and actively supervises it. It has specially formulated ten regulations for the Ministry of Interior to inspect the accounting of the Chinese Red Cross Society and specially appointed Mr. Pan Xulun, director of the Lixin Accounting Firm in this city, as the society's permanent auditor to handle matters in accordance with the promulgated regulations. It is understood that the Lixin Accounting Firm was previously entrusted by the Red Cross Society's board of directors to undertake the society's audit work for five years. The Ministry of Interior previously believed that the auditor should be appointed by the ministry, so the society terminated the original appointment of the accountant. However, because the Lixin Accounting Firm's audit work has always been serious, it was still appointed to this position. The ten inspection regulations are recorded below: (Ministry of Interior's Regulations for Inspecting the Accounting of the Red Cross Society of the Republic of China) 1. The Ministry of Interior has specially formulated these regulations in order to consolidate the financial foundation of the Red Cross Society of the Republic of China. 2. All accounting matters related to the inspection of the society as stipulated in these regulations shall be handled by a specially appointed accountant appointed by the ministry. 3. The inspection period shall be temporarily divided into four periods per year, each period lasting three months. Continuous inspection shall be carried out within each period. A concise report shall be issued within 15 days after the end of each period, and a detailed report for the entire year shall be issued within one month after the end of the year, and submitted to the ministry for review and approval. 4. The scope of inspection shall include all movable and immovable property, account books, vouchers, and related documents of the society. If temporarily designated by the ministry, the inspection shall be carried out in detail on the designated part. The foregoing inspection shall include the society's general headquarters and its affiliated first, second, and third hospitals, as well as other temporary agencies. 5. The points that should be paid special attention to during the implementation of the inspection are as follows: (A) Whether the preparation of all documents and account books of the society is appropriate and can reflect the society's entire true financial situation. (B) Whether all income and expenditure of the society are excessive or improper, and whether there is any violation or concealment of government laws and regulations and the society's accounting regulations. (D) Whether the society's accounting organization is sound. 6. The specially appointed accountant, after being designated by the ministry or entrusted by the society, may handle the following matters: (A) Various investigations, certifications, and appraisals. (B) Methods and procedures for preparing budgets and final accounts. (C) Methods for handling accounting matters and classification of accounting subjects. (D) The format of all accounting books, forms, bills, and vouchers. 7. In addition to the society's overall financial situation of property income and expenditure, the report shall include detailed explanations of the various items listed in Article 5 of these regulations. The contents of the foregoing report shall not be announced without the approval of the ministry. 8. The inspection fee of the specially appointed accountant shall be paid by the Red Cross Society of the Republic of China, and the amount shall be determined separately. 9. All accounting laws and regulations related to the society shall be copied and sent to the specially appointed accountant by the ministry or the society at any time for information. 10. All accounting inspection matters of the society in the 23rd year before the formulation of these regulations shall be handled in accordance with these regulations.

Grand Gathering of Engineers' Society at the International Hotel Before Opening 147

The Shanghai Branch of the Chinese Institute of Engineers holds a regular monthly meeting with lectures and dinners. The night before last (the 30th), with the new completion of the 22-story International Hotel in the new building of the Four Banks Joint Savings Society, a meeting was specially held in the hotel's restaurant. The members considered the building to be the tallest building in East Asia, and its engineering equipment was very impressive. They registered in advance and brought relatives and friends, totaling nearly 300 people. Before 7 o'clock, the members and their families who arrived at the meeting were shoulder to shoulder, and the threshold was blocked. After briefly visiting the magnificent and luxurious decorations, all of which were unprecedented, the guests were amazed. After taking their seats, the chairman, Mr. Xu Peihuang, first reported the purpose of the meeting and introduced Mr. Sa Fujun, the director of the Ministry of Railways, to give a lecture. Mr. Sa was ordered to go to Europe and the United States to inspect road administration, and described in detail the progress of transportation and the development and perfection of railway engineering in various European and American countries, which was extremely thorough. Next, Mr. Wu Daquan of the Four Banks Joint Savings Society was invited to speak. Mr. Wu said that since the opening of the sea ban and trade in China, there has been no institution in the country to treat international guests. Even Shanghai, which has the closest relationship, is the same. All the reception institutions for international guests are operated by foreigners. The colleagues have seen this and therefore spared no huge project to operate an international hotel to make up for this deficiency. Next, Mr. Qian Xinzhi was invited to speak. Mr. Qian explained that the association has been operating this large building for three years, and fortunately it has been completed. It cannot be said that it is not a major success in Chinese engineering. This 22-story building is 300 feet high and the foundation is 120 feet deep. The land price and construction cost 4.2 million yuan. All the projects are managed by various experts, without any slightness. Although the effort, time, and resources spent are many, the results obtained are satisfactory to all parties, and the colleagues are even more gratified. Now, to operate the hotel, funds are raised separately to establish a joint-stock limited company, organize a board of directors, and hire a manager to take full responsibility. From the financial perspective, investing in industry is the most stable business, and the progress of engineering relies on financial assistance. I sincerely hope that the financial and engineering circles will cooperate sincerely and unite to promote the progress of social undertakings, from an agricultural country to an industrial country. Next, Mr. Sun Liji, the architectural engineer of the association, reported the construction process. Mr. Wu Qingquan, the mechanical and electrical engineer of the association, reported the mechanical and electrical and sanitary fire-fighting equipment, which was very detailed. Finally, Vice-Chairman Wang Shengshan delivered a speech, saying that today, financiers and engineers are gathered together to enjoy a grand discussion, which is a very good phenomenon of mutual cooperation and is extremely gratifying. The operation and construction of the International Hotel has been very long, and the financial resources spent have been immeasurable. From the foundation laying to the completion, no work has been relaxed. This kind of down-to-earth business is by no means comparable to any speculative business, which shows the stability of the Four Banks Joint Savings Society in handling business. Our engineering circles are all optimistic about its success, and we will study and attack each other to expand the future of the engineering circles. After the meeting, it was 9:45 pm. The lights were turned on again, and the music began. The members began to dance socially, with hairpins and shadows, and the gathering was joyful. It ended at 10:30 pm.

It is heard that the British British American Tobacco Company (Limited Company) in China has recently organized two new companies, one is the British Yi Zhong Tobacco Co., Ltd., and the other is the British Yuan Zhong Tobacco Sales Co., Ltd. Shanghai Municipal Council Formulates Isolation Measures After Importing Cattle 154

The Shanghai Municipal Council has been implementing isolation measures for cattle in registered dairy farms for two years, which has been quite effective. However, there are no isolation facilities for cattle imported from overseas. Recently, a large number of cattle have been imported. If each dairy farm is allowed to handle it by itself, there is a risk of spreading diseases. The Director of the Health Department of the Shanghai Municipal Council therefore made a suggestion to the Health Committee that in the future, each factory must have a certificate from the veterinarian or other official agency of the place of origin when importing cattle, proving that there are no certain diseases prevalent in the area. After the Municipal Council's veterinarian inspects it again, the factory can pick it up. Generally, those who come from reliable places of origin and have certificates are generally safe. The isolation effect can also be achieved during the transportation period on large ships. However, in order to meet the needs of isolation after arriving in Shanghai, it is planned to temporarily use the upper floor of the slaughterhouse in the next few years, and at the same time, necessary precautions will be taken for meat products. This proposal was reviewed by the committee and referred to the Board of Directors for approval after consulting the veterinarian's report and statistics. The Board of Directors has already approved it on Wednesday.

Shanghai Municipal Council to Hold Rickshaw Puller Registration 155

Starting November 19

The Shanghai Municipal Council has decided to hold a registration for public rickshaw (yellow bag car) pullers starting on November 19. The registration locations are: 1. Hongkou, corner of Wusong Road and Bazilu; 2. Xinzha, workshop of the Public Works Department on Shunde Road (near Maigen Road Bridge). For each vehicle with a valid license owned by a public rickshaw registered owner, three rickshaw pullers can be recommended. When issuing the November license, the Municipal Council will also issue a recommendation form for each vehicle. The vehicle owner should select rickshaw pullers who are often hired and physically strong, and fill in the vehicle owner's name on the form. Vehicle owner's license number. Rickshaw puller's name. Age. Native place. Shanghai residence. etc. The rickshaw pullers should go to the registration place according to the location, date, and time specified on the form. The registration period is from November 19 to December 15. Also, if the recommendation form is lost, it will not be reissued. Holding a recommendation form does not necessarily mean that a rickshaw puller's license will be issued. It will still be issued after verification. The regulations for public rickshaw puller licenses have been seen in the Shanghai Municipal Council Gazette on July 18 and the newspapers on July 13.

Unfortunate Incident at Mainland Rubber Factory 158

Four People Burned

The Mainland Rubber Factory, located at No. 876 Taopeng Road, had an accident at about 11 am yesterday. When the factory workers were mixing hot cover oil and gasoline on the open space in the factory to prepare to paint rubber shoes, it happened that Mrs. Tang, a neighbor on the left, was also cooking next to the open space. Suddenly, a gust of wind carried the sparks from the stove into the gasoline pot. As a result, the pot caught fire immediately, and the flames soared. The workers Qian Heming, Zhao Yuexin, and Jiang Jinbao, who were working nearby, were burned by the gasoline first, and Mrs. Tang was also affected. Fortunately, the location was open, and the factory found out early, so it was put out immediately. However, the above four people were seriously injured, so the factory called the fire station and dispatched an ambulance to the Sacred Heart Hospital for treatment.

In the newly reclaimed areas of Huainan, ditches, roads, and wells are gradually being established in an orderly manner. The tenant farmers are increasingly numerous, all coming from other counties, with different languages, customs, and preferences. Therefore, a culture of mutual maintenance and assistance has not yet formed in their communal life. Recently, he initiated the establishment of a Buddhist Layman's Association, carefully constructing a Buddhist hall. He gathers his colleagues and leads the general tenant farmers to recite Buddhist scriptures during their spare time, without hindering their regular duties. This aims to establish a central belief for the new villagers in the coastal area. Mr. Zhu Jingci of the neighboring Dafeng Company strongly supports this initiative, purchasing a complete Song Dynasty Qisha Edition of the Buddhist Canon for the association, providing convenience for recitation and study. These two gentlemen advocate the Buddhist principles of charity and selflessness, aiming to save the world from the current rampant flood of selfishness. This is truly important. In the future, if Buddhification flourishes and other companies earnestly emulate them, farmers will yield field boundaries, travelers will yield the road, the folk customs will be simple and honest, and livelihoods will be rich and prosperous. People will regard the area as a paradise on earth and strive to return there.

Quit Smoking Without Pain and Continue Working as Usual.

Expansion of the Guangdong Sanatorium 162

Mr. Lu Yaocheng, an overseas Chinese, returned to China last year to visit his relatives. To offer preferential treatment to pregnant women, delivery is particularly affordable (only 5 yuan). Regarding birth control, if doctors deem that a woman should not have children, they will implement methods researched for over 20 years by the New York Birth Control Hospital in the United States, without any pain or danger. Closure of the Shanghai First Nursery 163

All Children Have Been Picked Up by Their Families.

A Labor Nursery Will Soon Be Established.

Shiye She reports that the Children's Welfare Committee, in order to promote the welfare of children, opened the First Nursery in March of this year. They secured a building in Yu Jia Nong, Xiao Nan Men, specifically for children under the age of six. The fees were divided into two levels: 7 yuan and 8 yuan. However, due to the limited space in the building, the nursery could only accommodate 50 children. Yang Rongmao, a specialist from the Shanghai Municipal Police Yizhong Supervision Office, served as the director in charge of the nursery's affairs. Since its establishment, the nursery has been operating for over half a year, and many people from all walks of life have been eager to send their children there. As a result, the quota was quickly filled, and more than a hundred people continued to register for a waiting list. It is reported that the nursery suddenly announced its closure yesterday and had already notified the families of the children in advance to come to the nursery, hold a meeting, and return the children to their families for self-care. As of yesterday, there were still nine children remaining at the nursery who hadn’t been picked up. In two cases, the families were not in Shanghai, so it was proposed to temporarily entrust the children to reliable hospitals for care. The Children's Welfare Committee, which is in charge of the nursery, will handle the aftermath properly and is also preparing to establish a labor nursery, which is expected to be established soon. It is initially planned to accept 30 children for a small-scale trial, with Li Ting'an, the director of the Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau, in charge of the nursery's affairs. Once funding is secured, it will be expanded.

American Sailors Seeking Revenge Are Warned and the Case Is Closed 171

The American Evening Post reports that yesterday morning (the 30th), several sailors from the American ship "General Pershing," docked in the Huangpu River, boarded the American ship "Cape Horn" to seek revenge. It is said that these men were all drunk, so they were easily driven away by the sailors of the "Cape Horn." These men were interrogated by American Consular Police Executive Corgill and the Public Works Department Police and Water Police officers at 4 p.m. when the "General Pershing" weighed anchor and returned to the ship. Subsequently, Corgill ordered the men to line up on the deck and sternly warned them that if they attempted to resolve their usual disputes with violence in Shanghai, they would be severely punished. This morning (the 31st), according to Corgill, American sailors are accustomed to resolving disputes related to unions, etc., after they leave their home country. They often believe that Shanghai is a suitable place to commit acts of violence, because they believe that Shanghai has consular jurisdiction, and they can escape the law after committing a crime.

Public Concession Begins Raising Roads 173

Preventing High Tide Inundation

The American Evening Post reports that due to the inconvenience caused by high tides in the Huangpu River during summer and autumn, when waves and muddy water rise and submerge the streets, the Public Works Department of the Municipal Council has begun a prevention plan. They will first raise Hankou Road between Sichuan Road and the Bund, which is most prone to flooding, by two chi. This work began two days ago, and they will then raise the Bund Road between Fuzhou Road and Hankou Road. This is because the section of the road has sunk due to the excessive pressure since the construction of the new Customs House. They will then gradually raise other low-lying areas. However, according to Public Works Department personnel, it is impossible to do so in many places unless the old houses are demolished and new houses with higher floors are built. To achieve a permanent solution, the outlet of the main ditch must be raised, but when it rains heavily, the water in the ditch cannot be easily discharged, and high-pressure pumps must be installed. This measure requires a huge expense, and it is impractical to install it for the flooding of a few places two or three times a year. Moreover, after new houses are rebuilt in the low-lying areas in the future, the roads will be raised accordingly, and the flooding problem will be solved naturally.

Special District to Draw 2,000 Rickshaw Licenses Starting Next Year 174

Approved for Operation by Minsheng Company

Xin Sheng She reports that the Public Concession Rickshaw Committee, previously in the name of helping rickshaw pullers, ordered rickshaw merchants to reduce the price of rickshaws. The company is named the Minsheng Rickshaw Company for the Relief of Rickshaw Pullers. In accordance with Article 16 of the Municipal Council's new regulations, it has requested the immediate extraction of 2,000 licenses for operation. The Rickshaw Committee has now approved this, and the allocation will begin on January 1, 24. The rickshaws will be built according to the Municipal Council's new rickshaw design. It has requested that charitable organizations allocate funds for construction. In addition to operating expenses, the remaining funds will be used to establish schools, provide educational materials, and operate hospitals. In addition to Shanghai, it will also be carried out in Jiangbei Yancheng, Dongtai, Taizhou, and other places one after another.

Calling It a Sino-Japanese Marine Products Intercourse Meeting

Nothing More Than the Vanguard of Economic Aggression Against China

Fraudulent Cohabitation Case 178

Wang Wenxiu Bitterly Complains

Fu Jianqing Provides a Reliable Guarantee

Fu Jianqing, a native of Suzhou, also known as Zhang Huai, a resident of No. 4 Hengmao Lane, Mintiniyin Road, Eight Immortals Bridge, French Concession, former director of the Second Branch of the Qingpu County Public Security Bureau, and current shareholder of Samsung Film Company, 36 years old this year, was recently sued in the Criminal Court of the Second Special District Court by Zhao Lingdi, also known as Wang Wenxiu, a native of Zhenjiang, 42 years old this year, the wife of the late Mr. Xi Jingui, a native of Dongting Mountain, formerly a senior scribe in the Public Works Department, residing at No. 16 Yuqing Lane, West Xinqiao Street, represented by lawyer Shen Shiyi, in accordance with Article 363 of the Criminal Code, for cohabiting under a false name, promising fraud, and taking property, requesting that the case be handled according to law, and attaching a civil suit to recover the defrauded money. The court accepted the complaint and specially opened the Criminal Court II yesterday morning, presided over by Judge Qiu Huan-ying, to summon both parties, each accompanied by their lawyers. First, the plaintiff, Zhao Lingdi, stated that her husband, Xi Jingui, had passed away eleven years ago, and she had been living in Xinping Lane, Longmen Road, determined to live a chaste life, relying on her husband's estate for a living. Last winter, she was introduced to the defendant by her neighbor, Old Woman Wang. The defendant was extremely tender and flattering, leading her to be seduced by him, and they began cohabiting in Hengmao Lane No. 30 at the end of last year. At first, she feared that he had ulterior motives and was always on guard, but his deception was extremely skillful. First, he invited her to lawyer Mao Xian's office to sign a cohabitation agreement. After that, he told her that the interest on the money she had deposited in the Hongkong and Shanghai Banking Corporation was too low, and it would be better to deposit it in the Huagan Trading Company, where she could get more generous interest. She believed him and handed over her seal to him. On February 24 of this year, she withdrew 1,273 yuan from her deposit in the Hongkong and Shanghai Banking Corporation and transferred 1,000 yuan to the Huawei Trading Company. The rest was taken by him through deception. When she questioned him, he replied that a husband and wife should not distinguish between each other and returned the deposit book to her for safekeeping. Later, he went to the north to seek employment and asked her for travel expenses, which she gave him in full. Unexpectedly, in July of this year, she fell ill and was bedridden. He said that he needed money to use and took away the deposit book, never to return. Suddenly, he filed a petition in the Civil Court to request that she be separated from the cohabitation relationship. In this situation, he knew that she had money in her bank account, and he wanted her to cohabit with him. Later, when he found out that she had no money, he wanted to break up with her. His conscience is so bad, it has caused her so much suffering, and she cannot survive. She requested the court to severely punish him according to law and force him to return the defrauded 1,000 yuan. The judge then questioned the defendant, Fu Jianqing, who stated that he had entered into a cohabitation relationship with the plaintiff on December 8 of last year, as proven by lawyers Qian and Mao. Later, he wanted to go to the north. She knew that he had a relationship with the prostitute Li Zhimei, also known as Huizhu, in Beiping, and would not allow him to go. She wanted him to issue a statement in the newspaper, severing the relationship with the prostitute Li, and at the same time, she wanted him to give her 1,000 yuan as a guarantee and give her 50 yuan a month for household expenses. He did everything. The 1,000 yuan deposited in the Huawei Trading Company was his own money, which he gave her as a guarantee, and it was not her property. On August 1 of this year, she suddenly left him and cohabited with her old lover, surnamed Liu, in Yuqing Lane. Therefore, he wanted to break up the cohabitation relationship with her. At this point, the judge asked the defendant, "You are 36 years old this year. Why did you cohabit with a 42-year-old widow? Do you love her for her looks or are you greedy for her money?" The defendant hesitated and could not answer. The court tentatively adjourned the hearing to November 19. The defendant was ordered to provide a reliable shop guarantee that he would appear whenever summoned, and if he could not provide a guarantee, he would be taken into custody.

The Public Utilities Bureau's Preparations for the Pudong Water Plant 179

The Municipal Government Entrusted the Xingye Trust Company to Handle

The Public Utilities Bureau Stopped the Preparations

The Public Utilities Bureau was ordered by the Municipal Government in May of the 19th year to prepare for the Pudong Water Plant. After actively formulating a plan, it was presented for approval. However, the required funding was more than 273,000 yuan. In addition to the 11,000 yuan allocated by the Finance Bureau for land purchase fees, the remaining 262,000 yuan was agreed upon with the Finance Bureau to allocate in installments, but the Finance Bureau found it difficult to raise the funds. Moreover, the January 28th Incident occurred, and it was forced to suspend temporarily. In the 21st year, the Municipal Government, due to the requests of the Municipal Party Department and Zhang Mingqin, the district chief of the Third District of the Public Security Bureau, to speed up the construction of the Pudong Water Plant, ordered the Public Utilities Bureau to submit a reply, requesting that the Finance Bureau be ordered to quickly allocate the funds for implementation according to the plan. However, the Finance Bureau had no funds to allocate, so it was suspended again. In the 22nd year, the Public Utilities Bureau planned to borrow funds from the Municipal Bank for implementation and submitted a report, which was reviewed by the Finance Bureau and was not approved. By the beginning of this year, the Public Utilities Bureau, because the demand for tap water from the citizens of Pudong was becoming more urgent, requested that the mayor invite gentlemen and merchants from the city to discuss implementation methods at the Bankers' Association and designated Lin Kanghou, Yao Mulian, Gui Yanfang, Pan Zhiwen, Chen Zixin, Zhang Xiaoliang, and Cai, the director of the Finance Bureau, and Xu, the director of the Public Utilities Bureau, as eight preparatory committee members. The Public Utilities Bureau convened a meeting of the preparatory committee members on March 15, and it was decided that the project would be jointly operated by the government and merchants. Merchant shares could raise 120,000 yuan, and government shares would be 80,000 yuan (including the assessed value of the land already purchased and allocated as the site for 30,000 yuan). The total amount of funds actually available was 170,000 yuan, which was still approximately 100,000 yuan short of the original difference of 262,000 yuan. The Public Utilities Bureau then negotiated with the Inland Tap Water Company, Zhabei Water and Electricity Company, and China Merchants Electric Company, etc., and they agreed to jointly contribute, with the reward money from the Inland Tap Water Company being used as collateral, to be amortized over five years starting from the 24th year. This plan was approved in principle by the Municipal Government upon submission by the Public Utilities Bureau. However, the Finance Bureau believed that the aforementioned amortization method would hinder the budget, so it was not established. Recently, the Public Utilities Bureau, in view of its responsibilities, believed that the establishment of the water plant could not be delayed any longer. After several deliberations, it found another way to raise funds, which would not interfere with the city's annual budget at all. It negotiated with Mr. Zhang Xiaoliang, a member of the preparatory committee, and decided to first advance the cost of starting construction and construct all the preparatory contracts and regulations for the water plant. The drawings and specifications of the relevant projects were sorted out and drafted, and a report was submitted to the Municipal Government for inspection and approval on October 18. The next day, it was ordered that the water plant be handled by the Xingye Trust Company. The Public Utilities Bureau replied that the funds for preparing the water plant were available and were already being actively implemented, so there was no need to entrust it to the Xingye Trust Company. On October 24, it convened a meeting of the preparatory committee to discuss matters relating to the implementation and the relevant regulations. At that time, all the committee members believed that the preparatory procedures for the water plant had been completed and unanimously decided that construction should be started immediately to ensure that the entire plant project would be completed and producing water by April next spring, supplying the citizens of Pudong. A report was made to the mayor, requesting that a meeting be convened as soon as possible to raise shares and formally establish the company. The matter was immediately handled according to the discussion, and the groundbreaking ceremony was scheduled for 3 p.m. on November 8. The water pipes, materials, water meters, Xiangpu motors, and contracting matters to be used in the water plant were also decided to be advertised for bids on October 31. At that time, the Public Utilities Bureau received a letter from the Secretariat of the Municipal Government transmitting the mayor's instructions that the water plant had been handed over to the Xingye Trust Company for handling, and the preparatory committee members should be informed immediately. In addition to notifying them as directed, all the completed preparations and construction of the water plant were immediately suspended.

Over one hundred yuan was found on their person

They specialized in picking customers' wallets

At 10:40 PM the night before, Officer Zhao Ziling of the Fuan Company Amusement Park on Dongmen Road in the Nanshi district, received a report. Another boy, Zhang Yinsheng (13 years old, from Songjiang, residing at No. 24, Donggou Yu Alley), was found with over thirty yuan in cash. Cow Bone Factory Chimney Attacked Case 181

The Er Yu Cow Bone Factory is operated by Japanese and located in Panjiawan, Zhabei, for nearly eight or nine years. The business is quite prosperous, but the internal equipment is very simple. The factory is surrounded by wasteland, where a group of Jiangbei poor people have built sheds and live there, no less than three hundred households. The day before (30th), at around 3:00 PM, sparks suddenly came out of the factory's iron chimney and fell on the thatched house built by Dai Hongxiang, a poor man from Jiangbei. This caused a fire to start immediately. Fortunately, it was daytime, so it was discovered and quickly extinguished, preventing a disaster. However, a group of poor people believed that the factory's chimney was too low, causing sparks to often fall on the thatched houses, leading to fires. They gathered in a corner, whispering privately. Before long, more and more people gathered, and the noise grew louder. They all wanted to make trouble for the factory. Some young troublemakers, without asking for any reason, broke the iron wire that held the chimney to the outside of the factory. But the chimney was old and worn out. Once it was pulled, it fell down along with the iron wire. The cement bricks below were also pulled down, destroying a corner of the factory's fence. At that time, the security team near the factory received the news and rushed to the scene, fearing a major disaster. They quickly notified the Tanziawan Police Station of the Xinzha Branch. Chief Li Qingjie of the station dispatched officers to suppress the situation. Because Dai Hongxiang and others still refused to be restrained, Dai, Zheng, Sun, and Jiang were all arrested, taken to the Xinzha Branch, and sent to the General Bureau for interrogation. A team was sent to investigate the truth. The factory owner also reported to the Japanese Consulate, which sent personnel yesterday to investigate with the Xinzha Branch District staff. It is said that the matter will be resolved soon.

Wife has no love and unwilling to be a burden

Court reconciles, both willing to divorce

Liu Rongdi, a Fujianese in his late 50s, residing at No. 28, Houjia House, Haige Road, Shanghai West, married Ms. Lu and has one son and two daughters. On the eighth day of the ninth month of the lunar calendar in the twentieth year of the Republic (1931), Chen Bingzhang, a local, introduced her to Cheng Jingxuan (26 years old), who lives at No. 3, Xiajiaqiao, Fahua East Town in this city, and works as a street vendor in the Hengxing Sock Factory near Jiumu Land on Minguo Road in the Nanshi district. The judge advised both parties to reconcile and granted the divorce. The plaintiff voluntarily abandoned all other claims.

Manager of China Industrial Bank Lu Mengxiang Arrested 183

Lu appointed manager after Qin Baoyuan fled

Promissory notes issued are never paid in cash

Will be tried together with Lu Xihou case

The China Industrial Bank went bankrupt, and the managing director Lu Xihou was investigated by the police and found that the savings deposits absorbed by the bank were obtained by Lu through improper business methods. A public prosecution for crimes such as fraud and embezzlement has been filed against Lu, and the First Special District Court has detained him for interrogation. Details were recorded in the previous report. It is now known that before the bank went bankrupt, its manager, Qin Baoyuan, fled with money on September 24. At that time, Lu Xihou believed that the position of manager could not be left vacant. He immediately promoted the bank's deputy manager, Lu Mengxiang, from Hangzhou, to the position so that he could be responsible to the outside world and maintain the bank's operations. However, after Lu took office, his attitude was the same as Qin Baoyuan, and his actions were also similar to Qin Baoyuan. Qin Baoyuan used to be directed by Lu Xihou, and for all payments that had to be made, he issued the bank's promissory notes, which were not honored when they were due. Lu Mengxiang was able to follow suit, also under the direction of Lu Xihou, and used promissory notes to stall. For example, on September 9, the Shen Bao newspaper had money deposited in the bank and issued a check for 1,150 yuan, which was handed over to the China-South Bank for collection. However, Lu Mengxiang, because there was no cash in the bank, and there was no reason to refuse payment, deliberately picked on it, deliberately provoking an argument with the person withdrawing the money, delaying the time. This trick was successful. The person withdrawing the money negotiated until 4:00 PM, and Lu Mengxiang finally agreed to pay the money, but said that it was past the prescribed business hours and could not be cashed. He then issued a promissory note for 1,150 yuan, stating that it was due on October 11. The person withdrawing the money had to take it back. On October 11, the bank suddenly went bankrupt, and the money was never recovered. Recently, the First Special District Court decided that anyone who wanted to sue the person in charge of the bank should report it to the police station so that it could be handled together. People holding the bank's dishonored notes or who were otherwise deceived reported to the General Police Station. The Shen Bao newspaper also sent this useless promissory note to the police station, asking them to investigate. It was determined that Lu Mengxiang was the manager when the note was issued, and he should be held jointly responsible with Lu Xihou for the deception. Xihou had already been detained for fraud. Mengxiang was arrested by the police at his home at No. 5, Xiaoshadu Road, the day before. He was taken to the First Special Court yesterday morning and interrogated by Judge Qian. After the police lawyer, Ru Baoyi, presented the case, he said that the defendant, Lu Mengxiang, had confessed to the police that he had signed the promissory note under the instigation of Lu Xihou. He requested that the case be postponed and tried together in the future. The defendant confessed that although he was appointed manager by Lu Xihou, Lu was still in charge of the manager position in reality. The defendant described the reasons for the dishonor of the 1,150 yuan promissory note and the procedures for issuing the note. Judge Qian said that his confession was quite different from what he had said when he testified in court when Lu Xihou was interrogated the other day. He then ordered him to confess truthfully and not to prevaricate. At that time, Wu Kejia, an employee of the Shanghai Bank, was also in court on business. Judge Qian wanted to investigate the situation of the promissory note and immediately called Wu to the case, ordering him to describe the procedures for issuing promissory notes by the bank so that it could be used as a reference. According to Wu's testimony, the procedures for issuing promissory notes depend on the size of the bank. For example, at the Shanghai Bank, it is not necessary for the managing director to know about the issuance of promissory notes. If the organization is smaller, the managing director is often stationed in the bank and can certainly know. Judge Qian then instructed the defendant Lu Mengxiang to pay a deposit of 10,000 yuan and postpone the trial to be combined with the Lu Xihou case.

Main culprit Bao La Xin escapes without a trace

Counterfeit Match Vouchers 185

Each thousand can be exchanged for seven yuan

Discovered early by tobacco company

Four people have been arrested so far

Recently, in order to compete for business, various tobacco companies in this city have been including gift vouchers in the boxes of cigarettes to attract customers. The Company Brand cigarettes issued by the Ruilun Tobacco Company on Kaifeng Road also include exchange vouchers, totaling more than 10 million. The most common is the match voucher. If you hold one voucher, you can exchange it for a box of matches at a nearby cigarette paper store. In order to take care of the cigarette paper stores, a flexible method was also established. If you accumulate 1,000 match vouchers, you can exchange them for seven yuan in cash from the company. This has been going on for several months since the issuance. Recently, the company suddenly discovered that someone outside was counterfeiting match vouchers and fraudulently claiming money from the company. It then notified employees to pay attention to the inspection. If they encountered the above situation, they would immediately detain them for investigation. The day before yesterday at around 3:00 PM, Zhang Zhilin from Zhenjiang brought 1,100 Company Brand match vouchers to Ruilun to exchange for cash. It was discovered that the vouchers were counterfeit. The Huishi Police Station was immediately notified, and detectives Ji Xiuquan and Giberson were dispatched to bring Zhang and the counterfeit vouchers to the police station. According to Zhang, the vouchers were given to him by Mi Guoxiang, who resides at No. 383, Huishan Road. After obtaining this information, the detectives went to the address to arrest Mi, but he had already fled. Only Mi's accomplice, Shi Pengcheng from Ningbo, was arrested. According to Shi, he used to be a printing broker. The vouchers were actually commissioned by Mi to be printed at the Wenhua Printing Factory at No. 120, Lane 914, Tangshan Road, totaling 120,000 vouchers. At that time, Mi took out 60 yuan for the printing fee, but he did not know the intention. The detectives then went to the Wenhua Printing Factory and arrested the owner, Wei Wenzheng, and brought him back to the police station. Since Wei did not know about the counterfeit vouchers beforehand, Wei was released, and Zhang and Shi were detained. Not long after, the Ruilun Tobacco Company brought Chen Shunrong from Ningbo and a 14-year-old Ningbo child, Jin Yuan, who held 2,000 vouchers and 2,600 vouchers respectively, all of which were counterfeit. The police station was notified and dispatched detectives to arrest them and detain them. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Eighth Criminal Court of the First Special Court. According to the police lawyer, Zhang Tianyin, there were many accomplices in this case, and the police are currently investigating. Therefore, he requested that Zhang, Shi, Tong, and Chen be detained first. He then presented the counterfeit vouchers to the court. According to Wang Xingtang, the manager of the Ruilun Company, the vouchers were confirmed to be counterfeit. When Zhang Zhilin was interrogated, he confessed that the vouchers were given to him by Mi Guoxiang to exchange for money from the company. He did not know they were counterfeit, so he had already paid Mi 6.5 yuan in advance. Shi Pengcheng also said that the vouchers were commissioned by Mi to be printed at the printing factory. Tong Jin Yuan said that he was an apprentice at the Xinchangtai Cigarette Paper Store on Xinmin Road, Zhabei. The vouchers were given to him by his master's wife to exchange for cash. Rong confessed that he lived on Wuzhou Road, but the vouchers were given to him by Ah Tang, a partner at the Rongshengchang Cigarette Paper Store opposite his residence, through Wu, and he did not know they were counterfeit. After Judge Wu Tingqi verified the confessions, he ordered Zhang and the other three to be detained for seven days for further interrogation.
